#PROJECT
PR:PROJECT_TITLE                 	Urinary Metabolites in IC/PBS Diagnosis
PR:PROJECT_TYPE                  	Disease
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	This West Coast Metabolomics Center sponsored pilot grant goal is to identify
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	and validate interstitial cystitis/painful bladder syndrome (IC/PBS)-associated
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	urinary metabolites. Our central hypothesis is that IC/PBS-associated
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	metabolites in the urine of IC/PBS patients can segregate patients from control
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	subjects, and that their levels are correlated with clinical symptoms. To test
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	this hypothesis, we will identify IC/PBS-associated metabolites in urine using
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	two independent platforms, GC-MS and quadrupole time-of-flight (Q-TOF) mass
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	spectrometry under the collaboration with UC Davis WCMC scientists. We believe
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	that this study will provide a significant potential clinical impact because
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	results may lead to clinical methods to increase diagnostic accuracy and an
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	improved understanding of the molecular basis of IC/PBS and its relationship to
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	urologic conditions with overlapping symptoms.
PR:INSTITUTE                     	University of California, Davis
PR:DEPARTMENT                    	Genome and Biomedical Sciences Facility
PR:LABORATORY                    	WCMC Metabolomics Core
PR:LAST_NAME                     	Fiehn
PR:FIRST_NAME                    	Oliver
PR:ADDRESS                       	Health Sciences Drive, Davis, California, 95616, USA
PR:EMAIL                         	ofiehn@ucdavis.edu
PR:PHONE                         	(530) 754-8258
PR:FUNDING_SOURCE                	NIH U24DK097154

#COLLECTION
CO:COLLECTION_SUMMARY            	All urine specimens were collected in the morning by clean catch methods.
CO:COLLECTION_SUMMARY            	Samples were centrifuged at 4◦C to remove cell debris, and supernatants were
CO:COLLECTION_SUMMARY            	aliquots of 1ml/tube, before storage at −80◦C until further analysis.
CO:SAMPLE_TYPE                   	Urine
#TREATMENT
TR:TREATMENT_SUMMARY             	Matched control urine vs. IC/PBS Urine
#SAMPLEPREP
SP:SAMPLEPREP_SUMMARY            	1. The dry sample is resuspended in 50 uL of Water/acetonitrile 95:5 containing
SP:SAMPLEPREP_SUMMARY            	100 ng/mL of CUDA (12-[[(cyclohexylamino)carbonyl]amino]-dodecanoic acid) as
SP:SAMPLEPREP_SUMMARY            	internal standard, vortexed for 10 sec, sonicated for 5 minutes, then
SP:SAMPLEPREP_SUMMARY            	centrifuged for 3 min at 14,000 rcf. 2. The samples are transferred to amber
SP:SAMPLEPREP_SUMMARY            	vials with micro-inserts and capped immediately, and stored at 4 degree C until
SP:SAMPLEPREP_SUMMARY            	and during analysis
SP:SAMPLEPREP_PROTOCOL_FILENAME  	SP_RP18_Protocol_KimUrine_IG102814.docx
